***idioom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:idioom.html>idioom</a> (64662)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">idiome</i>, and its source, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">idioma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἰδίωμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idíōma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a peculiarity, property, a peculiar phraseology, idiom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἰδιοῦσθαι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idioûsthai</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make one's own, appropriate to oneself</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἴδιος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ídios</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one's own, pertaining to oneself, private, personal, peculiar, separate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">idiom</span>, expression or a combination of <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> used in a language in a way which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> typical for that particular language</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:idool.html>idool</a> (15057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ydool</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">idole</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">idolum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εἴδωλον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eídōlon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">image, idol</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εἶδος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eîdos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">form</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:idool.html>idool</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:idolen.html>idolen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:idool.html>idooltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An idol, a statue or image that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the subject of worship.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afgod.html>afgod</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afgodsbeeld.html>afgodsbeeld</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>An idol <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> idolised</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">popidool</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">idolatrie</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>

***ie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a> (257)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely from earlier <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hi</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>Third-person singular, masculine, subjective, mute form:</i> he.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How does <b>he</b> do that?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely from unstressed <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Holland" class="extiw" title="w:Holland">Holland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>Second-person singular, mute form:</i> you.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krant.html>krant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelezen.html>gelezen</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Have <b>you</b> already read the newspaper?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Generally, this form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not used in Flanders, and in the Netherlands it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> largely restricted to <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> language.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">io</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> always, every time, continuously</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ever, sometime, at some point</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> entirely replaced by <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> like <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a></i> ("always, every time") and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a></i> ("ever, sometime, at some point") by the late 16th century.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Persoonlijk_voornaamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:persoonlijk.html>Persoonlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamwoord.html>voornaamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>Noord-Nederlands</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> clitische <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> 3e <a href = vnd.unilang:persoon.html>persoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkelvoud.html>enkelvoud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mannelijk.html>mannelijk</a> nominatief.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>Heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoed.html>hoed</a>?</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>

***ieder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ieder.html>ieder</a> (827)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ieder.html>ieder</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jeder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*iowether</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*iother</i>. A compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">io</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">always</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiw</i>) + <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wether</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whether</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwaþeraz</i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">either</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">jeder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ieder.html>ieder</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>each</li>
<li>any

<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">iewet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*iowiht</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ne</i> lt;lt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ne</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">io</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wiht</i> lt;lt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wihtą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:iet.html>iet</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>something, anything</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:iet.html>iet</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to any degree, in any way, at all</li>
<li>a little, somewhat</li>
<li>sometimes, perhaps</li></ol>
</body> 
***iets.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> (75)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:iet.html>iet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">iewet</i>, a contraction of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">iowiht</i>.
The Middle Dutch word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> formed out of the articles <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ie-</i> meaning 'anything', and a second article corresponding with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>wicht</a></i>, 'creature', of which its original meaning likely <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> 'thing'. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Limburgish" class="extiw" title="w:Limburgish">Limburgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="li">get</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Franconian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Central Franconian language">Central Franconian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-cfr">jet</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">aught</i>.
</p><p>In the word, the suffix -s <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> shaped under influence of the older <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a></i> wherein -s <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the ending of an old partitive genitive.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>something
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>Mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>?</i> : May it be something more?</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>Mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minder.html>minder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>?</i> : May it be something less?</dd></dl></li>
<li>anything
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:anders.html>Anders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a>?</i> : Anything else? (literally: Otherwise yet/still something?)</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ietsje.html>ietsje</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>somewhat</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beetje.html>beetje</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:enigszins.html>enigszins</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dichterbij.html>dichterbij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a>.</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a>.</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> prijzig.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ijdel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ijdel.html>ijdel</a> (11875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">idel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">īdil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*īdalaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">eitel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">idle</i>.
</p><p>The common Dutch loss of medial <i>-d-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a> to the by-forms <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijl.html>ijl</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:iel.html>iel</a></i>, which eventually acquired different meanings.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijdel.html>ijdel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijdel.html>ijdeler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ijdelst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vain, overly proud (of one's appearance, status etc.)</li>
<li>idle, in vain, unfounded</li>
<li>petty, <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>mere</a>, insignificant, worthless</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijdelheid.html>ijdelheid</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">ijdeltuit</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">verijdelen</span></li></ul>

***ijl.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ijl.html>ijl</a> (38182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contracted from late Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">idel</i>, which survives uncontracted as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijdel.html>ijdel</a></i>. An alternative contracted form <a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a> to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:iel.html>iel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijl.html>ijl</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijl.html>ijler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ijlst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rarefied (of a gas etc.), not dense</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> skinny, lacking fat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> empty</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">ijlheid</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***ijlen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ijlen.html>ijlen</a> (32579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijl.html>ijl</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">empty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, in phrases like <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ijlhoofdig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">empty-headed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijlen.html>ijlen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to rave, babble, maunder (speak quickly and incoherently as if one <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> delirious or mad)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ilen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">īlen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*īlijaną</i>. Derived from the noun <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*īlō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rush, haste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from which Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijl.html>ijl</a></i> with the same meaning.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijs.html>ijs</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsbeer.html>ijsbeer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsberen.html>ijsberen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsbeer.html>ijsbeertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***ijsberen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ijsberen.html>ijsberen</a> (17659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsbeer.html>ijsbeer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">polar bear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, from the behavior of polar <a href = vnd.unilang:bears.html>bears</a> in zoos.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsberen.html>ijsberen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pace back and forth
<ul><li><b>1999</b>, Jan amp; Marjorie <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Hartog, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vlucht.html>vlucht</a></i>, page 73.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schildwacht.html>schildwacht</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsbeerde.html>ijsbeerde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vlak.html>vlak</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buurt.html>buurt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vonk.html>vonk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verboden.html>verboden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sigaret.html>sigaret</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gloeide.html>gloeide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:donker.html>donker</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A sentry <b>paced to and fro</b> nearby, the spark of his prohibited cigarette sometimes lighted up in the dark.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ijsberg.html>ijsberg</a> (12092)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ijsberch</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijs.html>ijs</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:berg.html>berg</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mountain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***ijsco.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ijsco.html>ijsco</a> (42159)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsco.html>Ijsco</a></i>, clipping of <i>IJscompagnie</i> (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijs.html>ijs</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ice cream, ice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:compagnie.html>compagnie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">company</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), used for several ice cream companies in the Netherlands in the 1910s and 1920s (first in Amsterdam in 1913). First attested as a common noun in 1918.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsco.html>ijsco</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsco.html>ijsco</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsco.html>ijscootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> slightly dated  in some areas</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an <span class="Latn" lang="en">ice cream</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ijskast.html>ijskast</a> (10328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijs.html>ijs</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kast.html>kast</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cupboard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijskast.html>ijskast</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijskasten.html>ijskasten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijskastje.html>ijskastje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>refrigerator (originally a cupboard filled with ice to keep goods <a href = vnd.unilang:cool.html>cool</a>). <span class="defdate">[from mid/late 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li>ca. <b>1862</b>, "IJshandel", in <a href = vnd.unilang:oom.html>Oom</a> Diederik, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>Uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigen.html>eigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:vreemde.html>vreemde</a></i>, publ. by H. A. M. Roelants, page 116.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> „refrigerator”, d. i. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:draagbaar.html>draagbaar</a> ijshuis (<b><a href = vnd.unilang:ijskast.html>ijskast</a></b>) <a href = vnd.unilang:ontbreekt.html>ontbreekt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fatsoenlijk.html>fatsoenlijk</a> Amerikaan.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A "refrigerator", <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>.i. a portable coolhouse (<b>ice cupboard</b>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> never absent from the home of a respectable American.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>17th century or earlier. ***ijsthee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ijsthee.html>ijsthee</a> (12926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijs.html>ijs</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsthee.html>ijsthee</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsthee.html>ijstheeën</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> iced tea, ice tea <span class="defdate">[from mid 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1852</b>, J. J. A. Goeverneur, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:landen.html>Landen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:steden.html>steden</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:volken.html>volken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensch.html>menschen</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> panorama in <a href = vnd.unilang:negentien.html>negentien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groepen.html>groepen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 1, J. B. Wolters (publ.) page 62.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">iser</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*īsarn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*īsarną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*īsarnom</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁ésh₂r̥</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijzer.html>ijzer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">iron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vreter</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">devourer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijzervreter.html>ijzervreter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijzervreters.html>ijzervreters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijzervreter.html>ijzervretertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ijzervreetster</b>)
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tough, ruthless or relentless combative person, such as a hawk or a hard-ass.</li></ol>

***ik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> (2)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ic</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ek.html>ek</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*éǵh₂</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ich</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">I</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">jeg</i>.
See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">I</i> (English, etymology 3).<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:immer.html>immer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">always, ever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">adverb-forming suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:immers.html>immers</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Indicates that an explanation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> being given for an earlier statement.</span>; indeed, after all
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:immers.html>immers</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevraagd.html>gevraagd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>No, he's already home, <b>because</b> he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> asked to come home.</dd></dl></li>
<li>“<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Bataven" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Bataven">Bataven</a>” on the Dutch Wikipedia:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:tijdens.html>Tijdens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Nederlandse <a href = vnd.unilang:opstand.html>Opstand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Spaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:overheersing.html>overheersing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschouwden.html>beschouwden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Nederlanders <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:nakomelingen.html>nakomelingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Bataven', <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:immers.html>immers</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:onderdrukker.html>onderdrukkers</a>', <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Romeinen, in <a href = vnd.unilang:opstand.html>opstand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a>.
<dl><dd>During and after the Dutch Revolt against the Spanish domination, the Dutch regarded themselves as the 'descendants of the Batavians', <b>for</b> they <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> [<i>literally</i> who <b><a href = vnd.unilang:immers.html>immers</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a>] also come to rebel against their 'oppressors', the Romans.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
